    140 +  POUR: ['æ‰‹å†²', 'å•å“', 'pourover', 'æ»¤æ¯', 'äº§åŒº'],
    141 +  DESSERT: ['ç”œå“', 'dessert', 'è›‹ç³•', 'ç”œ', 'èŠå£«', 'ç‚¹å¿ƒ']
    142 +}
    143 +const categoryOrder = ['CLASSIC', 'SIGNATURE', 'POUR', 'DESSERT']
    144 +
    145 +const normalizedCategory = computed(() => props.activeCategory || 'CLASSIC')
    146 +
    147 +const resolveCategory = (drink, index) => {
    148 +  const explicit = String(drink.category || drink.type || '').toUpperCase()
    149 +  if (categoryOrder.includes(explicit)) return explicit
    150 +  const text = `${drink.name} ${drink.flavorProfile || ''} ${drink.description || ''}`.toLowerCase()
    151 +  for (const [category, keywords] of Object.entries(keywordMap)) {
    152 +    if (keywords.some((word) => text.includes(word.toLowerCase()))) {
    153 +      return category
    154 +    }
    155 +  }
    156 +  return categoryOrder[index % categoryOrder.length]
    157 +}
    158 +
    159 +const enrichedDrinks = computed(() =>
    160 +  props.drinks.map((drink, index) => ({
    161 +    ...drink,
    162 +    __key: String(drink.id),
    163 +    __category: resolveCategory(drink, index)
    164 +  }))
    165 +)
    166 +
    167 +const visibleDrinks = computed(() =>
    168 +  enrichedDrinks.value.filter((drink) => drink.__category === normalizedCategory.value)
    169 +)
    170 +
    171 +const categoryHeading = computed(() => `${props.categoryLabel}çµæ„Ÿå•`)
    172 +const introCopy = computed(() => `åœ¨ ${props.categoryLabel} åˆ†ç±»ä¸­éšå¿ƒç‚¹å•ï¼Œç‚¹äº®ä½ çš„æ™¨é—´çµæ„Ÿã€‚`)
    173 +
    174 +const cartItems = computed(() =>
    175 +  Object.entries(cart)
    176 +    .map(([id, meta]) => {
    177 +      const drink = enrichedDrinks.value.find((item) => item.__key === id)
    178 +      if (!drink) return null
    179 +      return {
    180 +        id: drink.id,
    181 +        name: drink.name,
    182 +        price: drink.price,
    183 +        merchantName: drink.merchantName,
    184 +        quantity: meta.quantity
    185 +      }
    186 +    })
    187 +    .filter(Boolean)
    188 +)
    189 +
    190 +const cartCount = computed(() => cartItems.value.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.quantity, 0))
    191 +const cartTotal = computed(() =>
    192 +  cartItems.value.reduce((sum, item) => sum + Number(item.price || 0) * item.quantity, 0)
    193 +)
    194 +
    195 +const submitLabel = computed(() => {
    196 +  if (submitting.value) return 'é¢„çº¦ä¸­...'
    197 +  if (!cartItems.value.length) return 'è¯·å…ˆæ·»åŠ é¥®å“'
    198 +  return `æäº¤ ${cartCount.value} æ¯`
    199 +})
    200 +
    201 +const increment = (drink) => {
    202 +  const key = String(drink.id)
    203 +  if (!cart[key]) {
    204 +    cart[key] = { quantity: 1 }
    205 +    return
    206 +  }
    207 +  cart[key].quantity += 1
    208 +}
    209 +
    210 +const decrement = (drink) => {
    211 +  const key = String(drink.id)
    212 +  if (!cart[key]) return
    213 +  cart[key].quantity -= 1
    214 +  if (cart[key].quantity <= 0) {
    215 +    delete cart[key]
    216 +  }
    217 +}
    218 +
    219 +const incrementById = (drinkId) => {
    220 +  const drink = enrichedDrinks.value.find((item) => item.id === drinkId)
    221 +  if (drink) increment(drink)
    222 +}
    223 +
    224 +const decrementById = (drinkId) => {
    225 +  const drink = enrichedDrinks.value.find((item) => item.id === drinkId)
    226 +  if (drink) decrement(drink)
    227 +}
    228 +
    229 +const clearCart = () => {
    230 +  Object.keys(cart).forEach((key) => delete cart[key])
    231 +  cartOpen.value = false
    232 +}
    233 +
    234 +const toggleCart = () => {
    235 +  if (!cartItems.value.length) return
    236 +  cartOpen.value = !cartOpen.value
    237 +}
    238 +
    239 +watch(
    240 +  () => props.merchants,
    241 +  (list) => {
    242 +    if (!form.merchantId && list.length) {
    243 +      form.merchantId = list[0].id
    244 +    } else if (form.merchantId && !list.some((merchant) => merchant.id === form.merchantId)) {
    245 +      form.merchantId = list[0]?.id || ''
    246 +    }
    247 +  },
    248 +  { immediate: true }
    249 +)
    250 +
    251 +watch(
    252 +  () => enrichedDrinks.value.map((drink) => drink.__key),
    253 +  (keys) => {
    254 +    const validIds = new Set(keys)
    255 +    Object.keys(cart).forEach((key) => {
    256 +      if (!validIds.has(key)) {
    257 +        delete cart[key]
    258 +      }
    259 +    })
    260 +  },
    261 +  { immediate: true }
    262 +)
    263 +
    264 +watch(
    265 +  () => cartItems.value.length,
    266 +  (count) => {
    267 +    if (!count) {
    268 +      cartOpen.value = false
    269 +    }
    270 +  }
    271 +)
    272 +
    273 +watch(
    274 +  () => cartItems.value,
    275 +  (items) => {
    276 +    emit('cart-change', { items, count: cartCount.value, total: cartTotal.value })
    277 +  },
    278 +  { deep: true, immediate: true }
    279 +)
    280 +
    281 +const withVisual = (image) => {
    282 +  if (!image)
    283 +    return 'background-image: linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(56, 189, 248, 0.28), rgba(30, 64, 175, 0.32));'
    284 +  return `background-image: url(${image});`
    285 +}
    286 +
    287 +const handleSubmit = async () => {
    288 +  if (!cartItems.value.length) {
    289 +    message.value = 'è¯·å…ˆé€‰æ‹©è‡³å°‘ä¸€æ¯é¥®å“'
    290 +    success.value = false
    291 +    return
    292 +  }
    293 +
    294 +  submitting.value = true
    295 +  message.value = ''
    296 +  success.value = false
    297 +
    298 +  try {
    299 +    await props.submitOrder({
    300 +      customerName: form.customerName,
    301 +      contactPhone: form.contactPhone,
    302 +      merchantId: form.merchantId,
    303 +      pickupTime: form.pickupTime,
    304 +      items: cartItems.value.map((item) => ({ drinkId: item.id, quantity: item.quantity }))
    305 +    })
    306 +    Object.assign(form, initialState())
    307 +    clearCart()
    308 +    message.value = 'é¢„çº¦æˆåŠŸï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä¼šåœ¨åˆ¶ä½œå®ŒæˆåçŸ­ä¿¡æé†’ä½ ã€‚'
    309 +    success.value = true
    310 +  } catch (error) {
    311 +    message.value = error?.response?.data?.message || 'ä¸‹å•å¤±è´¥ï¼Œè¯·ç¨åé‡è¯•ã€‚'
    312 +  } finally {
    313 +    submitting.value = false
    314 +  }
    315 +}
    316 +
    317 +defineExpose({
    318 +  incrementById,
    319 +  decrementById,
    320 +  clearCart
    321 +})
    322 +</script>

     97 +              <p>{{ drink.description || 'è¿™æ¯é¥®å“è¿˜åœ¨ç­‰ä½ æ¥å®šä¹‰é£å‘³æ•…äº‹ã€‚' }}</p>
     98 +              <div class="menu-item-meta">
     99 +                <span class="menu-price">Â¥ {{ Number(drink.price).toFixed(2) }}</span>
    100 +                <span class="menu-merchant">{{ drink.merchantName || 'å®éªŒå®¤è‡ªè¥' }}</span>
    101 +              </div>
    102 +            </div>
    103 +            <div class="menu-item-actions">
    104 +              <button type="button" class="circle" :disabled="!cart[String(drink.id)]" @click="decrement(drink)
         ">
    105 +                -
    106 +              </button>
    107 +              <span>{{ cart[String(drink.id)]?.quantity || 0 }}</span>
    108 +              <button type="button" class="circle primary" @click="increment(drink)">+</button>
    109 +            </div>
    110 +          </li>
    111 +        </ul>
    112 +      </div>
    113 +      <div v-else class="empty-state">
    114 +        <h2>æš‚æœªä¸Šæ¶è¯¥åˆ†ç±»</h2>
    115 +        <p>å¯åˆ‡æ¢åˆ°å…¶ä»–åˆ†ç±»ï¼Œæˆ–ç¨åå…³æ³¨æ–°å“ä¸Šçº¿ã€‚</p>
    116 +      </div>
    117 +
    118 +      <div class="cart-panel" :class="{ open: cartOpen }">
    119 +        <button type="button" class="cart-toggle" :disabled="!cartItems.length" @click="toggleCart">
    120 +          <div class="cart-icon">
    121 +            <span>{{ cartCount }}</span>
    122 +          </div>
    123 +          <div class="cart-brief">
    124 +            <strong>{{ cartItems.length ? `å·²é€‰ ${cartCount} æ¯` : 'è´­ç‰©è½¦ä¸ºç©º' }}</strong>
    125 +            <small>{{ cartItems.length ? 'å¯åœ¨å³ä¾§è°ƒæ•´æ¯æ•°' : 'ä»ä¸Šæ–¹èœå•åŠ å…¥å•†å“' }}</small>
    126 +          </div>
    127 +          <span class="cart-total">Â¥ {{ cartTotal.toFixed(2) }}</span>
    128 +          <span class="cart-chevron" :class="{ rotated: cartOpen }">â–¾</span>
    129 +        </button>
    130 +        <div class="cart-body" v-if="cartOpen">
    131 +          <div class="cart-head">
    132 +            <span>è´­ç‰©è½¦</span>
    133 +            <button type="button" class="ghost" @click="clearCart">æ¸…ç©º</button>
    134 +          </div>
    135 +          <ul v-if="cartItems.length">
    136 +            <li v-for="item in cartItems" :key="item.id" class="cart-item">
    137 +              <div>
    138 +                <h4>{{ item.name }}</h4>
    139 +                <p>Â¥ {{ Number(item.price).toFixed(2) }}</p>
    140 +              </div>
    141 +              <div class="menu-item-actions">
    142 +                <button type="button" class="circle" @click="decrement(item)">-</button>
    143 +                <span>{{ item.quantity }}</span>
    144 +                <button type="button" class="circle primary" @click="increment(item)">+</button>
    145 +              </div>
    146 +            </li>
    147 +          </ul>
    148 +          <p v-else class="cart-empty">è´­ç‰©è½¦æš‚æ—¶æ²¡æœ‰å†…å®¹</p>
    149 +        </div>
    150 +      </div>
    151 +    </template>
    152 +
    153 +    <form class="order-form" @submit.prevent="handleSubmit">
    154 +      <div class="field">
    155 +        <label for="customer">ç§°å‘¼</label>
    156 +        <input id="customer" v-model="form.customerName" type="text" placeholder="å¦‚ï¼šæ™¨å…‰" required />
    157 +      </div>
    158 +      <div class="field">
    159 +        <label for="phone">è”ç³»ç”µè¯</label>
    160 +        <input id="phone" v-model="form.contactPhone" type="tel" placeholder="è¯·è¾“å…¥æ‰‹æœºå·" required />
    161 +      </div>
    162 +      <div class="field">
    163 +        <label for="merchant">å–æ¯é—¨åº—</label>
    164 +        <select id="merchant" v-model="form.merchantId" required>
    165 +          <option disabled value="">é€‰æ‹©é—¨åº—</option>
    166 +          <option v-for="merchant in merchants" :key="merchant.id" :value="merchant.id">
    167 +            {{ merchant.name }} Â· {{ merchant.location }}
    168 +          </option>
    169 +        </select>
    170 +      </div>
    171 +      <div class="field">
    172 +        <label for="pickup">é¢„è®¡å–æ¯æ—¶é—´</label>
    173 +        <input id="pickup" v-model="form.pickupTime" type="time" />
    174 +      </div>
    175 +      <button :disabled="submitting || !cartItems.length">
    176 +        {{ submitLabel }}
    177 +      </button>
    178 +      <p v-if="!cartItems.length" class="cart-hint">è¯·å…ˆé€šè¿‡åˆ†ç±»èœå•åŠ å…¥è‡³å°‘ä¸€æ¯é¥®å“</p>
    179 +      <p v-if="message" class="message" :class="{ 'message--success': success }">{{ message }}</p>
    180 +    </form>
    181 +  </section>
    182 +</template>
    183 +
    184 +<script setup>
    185 +import { computed, reactive, ref, watch } from 'vue'
    186 +
    187 +const props = defineProps({
    188 +  drinks: { type: Array, default: () => [] },
    189 +  merchants: { type: Array, default: () => [] },
    190 +  submitOrder: { type: Function, required: true },
    191 +  activeCategory: { type: String, default: 'CLASSIC' },
    192 +  categoryLabel: { type: String, default: 'ç»å…¸' }
    193 +})
    194 +
    195 +const emit = defineEmits(['cart-change', 'navigate-category'])
    196 +
    197 +const initialState = () => ({
    198 +  customerName: '',
    199 +  contactPhone: '',
    200 +  merchantId: '',
    201 +  pickupTime: ''
    202 +})
    203 +
    204 +const form = reactive(initialState())
    205 +const submitting = ref(false)
    206 +const message = ref('')
    207 +const success = ref(false)
    208 +const cart = reactive({})
    209 +const cartOpen = ref(false)
    210 +
    211 +const dessertNavItems = [
    212 +  { id: 'dessert', label: 'ç”œå“', category: 'DESSERT' },
    213 +  { id: 'classic', label: 'ç»å…¸å’–å•¡', category: 'CLASSIC' },
    214 +  { id: 'pour', label: 'ç‰¹è‰²æ‰‹å†²', category: 'POUR' },
    215 +  { id: 'signature', label: 'ç‰¹è°ƒ', category: 'SIGNATURE' }
    216 +]
    217 +
    218 +const dessertShowcase = [
    219 +  {
    220 +    id: 'fig-basque',
    221 +    anchor: 'fig',

    224 +    price: 48,
    225 +    tag: 'é™å®šä¸Šæ–°',

    228 +  },
    229 +  {

    233 +    description: '70% é»‘å·§ä¸æ¤°æ£ç³–æµ†å åŠ ï¼Œå…¥å£ä¸æ»‘å¸¦æœ‰æ²™æ¼ é¦™æ–™æ°”æ¯ã€‚',
    234 +    price: 52,
    235 +    tag: 'ä¸­ä¸œçµæ„Ÿ',
    236 +    image: 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1505253399886-34b28f31c15f?auto=format&fit=crop&w=400&q=80',
    237 +    background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.15), rgba(249, 115, 22, 0.15))'
    238 +  },
    239 +  {
    240 +    id: 'matcha-brownie',
    241 +    anchor: 'matcha',
    242 +    name: 'æŠ¹èŒ¶å¸ƒæœ—å°¼å·´æ–¯å…‹',
    243 +    description: 'å®‡æ²»æŠ¹èŒ¶ä¸å¯å¯å¸ƒæœ—å°¼çš„åŒå±‚ç»“æ„ï¼Œå›å‘³æœ‰æ˜æ˜¾åšæœé¦™ã€‚',
    244 +    price: 46,
    245 +    tag: 'äº¬éƒ½ x å¸ƒæœ—å°¼',
    246 +    image: 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1470337458703-46ad1756a187?auto=format&fit=crop&w=400&q=80',
    247 +    background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.18), rgba(8, 47, 73, 0.35))'
    248 +  },
    249 +  {
    250 +    id: 'lemon-cheese',
    251 +    anchor: 'lemon',
    252 +    name: 'æŸ æª¬ä¹³é…ªå·´æ–¯å…‹',
    253 +    description: 'è¥¿è¥¿é‡ŒæŸ æª¬çš®ä¸é’æŸ æ±è°ƒé…¸ï¼Œè¡¨é¢è–„è„†å¾®ç„¦ï¼Œé€‚åˆå¤æ—¥æ¸…çˆ½å£æ„Ÿã€‚',
    254 +    price: 45,
    255 +    tag: 'å¤æ—¥ç²¾é€‰',
    256 +    image: 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1481391032119-d89fee407e44?auto=format&fit=crop&w=400&q=80',
    257 +    background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(251, 191, 36, 0.2), rgba(248, 250, 252, 0.08))'
    258 +  }
    259 +]
    260 +
    261 +const keywordMap = {
    262 +  CLASSIC: ['ç»å…¸', 'æ‹¿é“', 'ç¾å¼', 'latte', 'americano'],
    263 +  SIGNATURE: ['ç‰¹è°ƒ', 'çµæ„Ÿ', 'é™å®š', 'signature', 'åˆ›æ„', 'è”å'],
    264 +  POUR: ['æ‰‹å†²', 'å•å“', 'pourover', 'æ»¤æ¯', 'äº§åŒº'],
    265 +  DESSERT: ['ç”œå“', 'dessert', 'è›‹ç³•', 'å·´æ–¯å…‹', 'èŠå£«', 'ç‚¹å¿ƒ']
    266 +}
    267 +const categoryOrder = ['CLASSIC', 'SIGNATURE', 'POUR', 'DESSERT']
    268 +
    269 +const normalizedCategory = computed(() => props.activeCategory || 'CLASSIC')
    270 +const isDessert = computed(() => normalizedCategory.value === 'DESSERT')
    271 +
    272 +const resolveCategory = (drink, index) => {
    273 +  const explicit = String(drink.category || drink.type || '').toUpperCase()
    274 +  if (categoryOrder.includes(explicit)) return explicit
    275 +  const text = `${drink.name} ${drink.flavorProfile || ''} ${drink.description || ''}`.toLowerCase()
    276 +  for (const [category, keywords] of Object.entries(keywordMap)) {
    277 +    if (keywords.some((word) => text.includes(word.toLowerCase()))) {
    278 +      return category
    279 +    }
    280 +  }
    281 +  return categoryOrder[index % categoryOrder.length]
    282 +}
    283 +
    284 +const enrichedDrinks = computed(() =>
    285 +  props.drinks.map((drink, index) => ({
    286 +    ...drink,
    287 +    __key: String(drink.id),
    288 +    __category: resolveCategory(drink, index)
    289 +  }))
    290 +)
    291 +
    292 +const visibleDrinks = computed(() =>
    293 +  enrichedDrinks.value.filter((drink) => drink.__category === normalizedCategory.value)
    294 +)
    295 +
    296 +const dessertProducts = computed(() =>
    297 +  dessertShowcase.map((item) => {
    298 +    const drink = enrichedDrinks.value.find(
    299 +      (entry) => entry.name?.includes(item.name) || item.name.includes(entry.name || '')
    300 +    )
    301 +    return { ...item, drink }
    302 +  })
    303 +)
    304 +
    305 +const dessertNavMap = {
    306 +  dessert: { anchor: 'dessert-must' },
    307 +  classic: { category: 'CLASSIC' },
    308 +  pour: { category: 'POUR' },
    309 +  signature: { category: 'SIGNATURE' }
    310 +}
    311 +
    312 +const categoryHeading = computed(() => `${props.categoryLabel}çµæ„Ÿå•`)
    313 +const introCopy = computed(() => `åœ¨ ${props.categoryLabel} åˆ†ç±»ä¸­éšå¿ƒç‚¹å•ï¼Œç‚¹äº®ä½ çš„æ™¨é—´çµæ„Ÿã€‚`)
    314 +
    315 +const cartItems = computed(() =>
    316 +  Object.entries(cart)
    317 +    .map(([id, meta]) => {
    318 +      const drink = enrichedDrinks.value.find((item) => item.__key === id)
    319 +      if (!drink) return null
    320 +      return {
    321 +        id: drink.id,
    322 +        name: drink.name,
    323 +        price: drink.price,
    324 +        merchantName: drink.merchantName,
    325 +        quantity: meta.quantity
    326 +      }
    327 +    })
    328 +    .filter(Boolean)
    329 +)
    330 +
    331 +const cartCount = computed(() => cartItems.value.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.quantity, 0))
    332 +const cartTotal = computed(() =>
    333 +  cartItems.value.reduce((sum, item) => sum + Number(item.price || 0) * item.quantity, 0)
    334 +)
    335 +const cartSummaryText = computed(() =>
    336 +  cartItems.value.length ? `å·²é€‰ ${cartCount.value} ä»¶ Â· Â¥${cartTotal.value.toFixed(2)}` : 'è´­ç‰©è½¦ä¸ºç©º'
    337 +)
    338 +
    339 +const submitLabel = computed(() => {
    340 +  if (submitting.value) return 'é¢„çº¦ä¸­...'
    341 +  if (!cartItems.value.length) return 'è¯·å…ˆæ·»åŠ é¥®å“'
    342 +  return `æäº¤ ${cartCount.value} æ¯`
    343 +})
    344 +
    345 +const increment = (drink) => {
    346 +  const key = String(drink.id)
    347 +  if (!cart[key]) {
    348 +    cart[key] = { quantity: 1 }
    349 +    return
    350 +  }
    351 +  cart[key].quantity += 1
    352 +}
    353 +
    354 +const decrement = (drink) => {
    355 +  const key = String(drink.id)
    356 +  if (!cart[key]) return
    357 +  cart[key].quantity -= 1
    358 +  if (cart[key].quantity <= 0) {
    359 +    delete cart[key]
    360 +  }
    361 +}
    362 +
    363 +const incrementById = (drinkId) => {
    364 +  const drink = enrichedDrinks.value.find((item) => item.id === drinkId)
    365 +  if (drink) increment(drink)
    366 +}
    367 +
    368 +const decrementById = (drinkId) => {
    369 +  const drink = enrichedDrinks.value.find((item) => item.id === drinkId)
    370 +  if (drink) decrement(drink)
    371 +}
    372 +
    373 +const addDessert = (product) => {
    374 +  if (!product.drink) return
    375 +  increment(product.drink)
    376 +}
    377 +
    378 +const clearCart = () => {
    379 +  Object.keys(cart).forEach((key) => delete cart[key])
    380 +  cartOpen.value = false
    381 +}
    382 +
    383 +const toggleCart = () => {
    384 +  if (!cartItems.value.length) return
    385 +  cartOpen.value = !cartOpen.value
    386 +}
    387 +
    388 +const scrollDessert = (nav) => {
    389 +  const target = dessertNavMap[nav.id]
    390 +  if (!target) return
    391 +  if (target.category && target.category !== 'DESSERT') {
    392 +    emit('navigate-category', target.category)
    393 +  } else if (target.anchor) {
    394 +    const el = document.getElementById(target.anchor)
    395 +    el?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' })
    396 +  }
    397 +}
    398 +
    399 +watch(
    400 +  () => props.merchants,
    401 +  (list) => {
    402 +    if (!form.merchantId && list.length) {
    403 +      form.merchantId = list[0].id
    404 +    } else if (form.merchantId && !list.some((merchant) => merchant.id === form.merchantId)) {
    405 +      form.merchantId = list[0]?.id || ''
    406 +    }
    407 +  },
    408 +  { immediate: true }
    409 +)
    410 +
    411 +watch(
    412 +  () => enrichedDrinks.value.map((drink) => drink.__key),
    413 +  (keys) => {
    414 +    const validIds = new Set(keys)
    415 +    Object.keys(cart).forEach((key) => {
    416 +      if (!validIds.has(key)) {
    417 +        delete cart[key]
    418 +      }
    419 +    })
    420 +  },
    421 +  { immediate: true }
    422 +)
    423 +
    424 +watch(
    425 +  () => cartItems.value.length,
    426 +  (count) => {
    427 +    if (!count) {
    428 +      cartOpen.value = false
    429 +    }
    430 +  }
    431 +)
    432 +
    433 +watch(
    434 +  () => cartItems.value,
    435 +  (items) => {
    436 +    emit('cart-change', { items, count: cartCount.value, total: cartTotal.value })
    437 +  },
    438 +  { deep: true, immediate: true }
    439 +)
    440 +
    441 +const withVisual = (image) => {
    442 +  if (!image)
    443 +    return 'background-image: linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(56, 189, 248, 0.28), rgba(30, 64, 175, 0.32));'
    444 +  return `background-image: url(${image});`
    445 +}
    446 +
    447 +const handleSubmit = async () => {
    448 +  if (!cartItems.value.length) {
    449 +    message.value = 'è¯·å…ˆé€‰æ‹©è‡³å°‘ä¸€æ¯é¥®å“'
    450 +    success.value = false
    451 +    return
    452 +  }
    453 +
    454 +  submitting.value = true
    455 +  message.value = ''
    456 +  success.value = false
    457 +
    458 +  try {
    459 +    await props.submitOrder({
    460 +      customerName: form.customerName,
    461 +      contactPhone: form.contactPhone,
    462 +      merchantId: form.merchantId,
    463 +      pickupTime: form.pickupTime,
    464 +      items: cartItems.value.map((item) => ({ drinkId: item.id, quantity: item.quantity }))
    465 +    })
    466 +    Object.assign(form, initialState())
    467 +    clearCart()
    468 +    message.value = 'é¢„çº¦æˆåŠŸï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä¼šåœ¨åˆ¶ä½œå®ŒæˆåçŸ­ä¿¡æé†’ä½ ã€‚'
    469 +    success.value = true
    470 +  } catch (error) {
    471 +    message.value = error?.response?.data?.message || 'ä¸‹å•å¤±è´¥ï¼Œè¯·ç¨åé‡è¯•ã€‚'
    472 +  } finally {
    473 +    submitting.value = false
    474 +  }
    475 +}
    476 +
    477 +defineExpose({
    478 +  incrementById,
    479 +  decrementById,
    480 +  clearCart
    481 +})
    482 +</script>

     96 +const categoryOrder = ['CLASSIC', 'SIGNATURE', 'POUR', 'DESSERT']
     97 +
     98 +const resolveCategory = (drink, index) => {
     99 +  const explicit = String(drink.category || drink.type || '').toUpperCase()
    100 +  if (categoryOrder.includes(explicit)) return explicit
    101 +  const text = `${drink.name} ${drink.flavorProfile || ''} ${drink.description || ''}`.toLowerCase()
    102 +  for (const [category, keywords] of Object.entries(keywordMap)) {
    103 +    if (keywords.some((word) => text.includes(word.toLowerCase()))) {
    104 +      return category
    105 +    }
    106 +  }
    107 +  return categoryOrder[index % categoryOrder.length]
    108 +}

     95 +const activeSection = ref(props.initialCategory || 'CLASSIC')

     97 +const resolveCategory = (drink, index) => {
     98 +  const explicit = String(drink.category || drink.type || '').toUpperCase()
     99 +  if (categoryOrder.includes(explicit)) return explicit
    100 +  const text = `${drink.name} ${drink.flavorProfile || ''} ${drink.description || ''}`.toLowerCase()

    184 +const resolveCategory = (drink, index) => {

     95 +]
     96 +
     97 +const activeCategory = ref(props.initialCategory || 'CLASSIC')
     98 +const contentRef = ref(null)
     99 +const cart = reactive({})
    100 +
    101 +const resolveCategory = (drink, index) => {
    102 +  const explicit = String(drink.category || drink.type || '').toUpperCase()
    103 +  if (navItems.some((item) => item.value === explicit)) return explicit
    104 +  const text = `${drink.name} ${drink.description || ''}`.toLowerCase()
    105 +  if (text.includes('æ‰‹å†²')) return 'POUR'
    106 +  if (text.includes('ç‰¹è°ƒ')) return 'SIGNATURE'
    107 +  return navItems[index % navItems.length].value
    108 +}
    109 +
    110 +const sections = computed(() =>
    111 +  navItems.map((item) => ({
    112 +    ...item,
    113 +    anchor: `section-${item.value.toLowerCase()}`,
    114 +    items: props.drinks.filter((drink, index) => resolveCategory(drink, index) === item.value)
    115 +  }))
    116 +)
    117 +
    118 +const cartItems = computed(() => Object.values(cart))
    119 +const cartTotal = computed(() =>
    120 +  cartItems.value.reduce((sum, item) => sum + Number(item.price || 0) * item.quantity, 0)
    121 +)
    122 +
    123 +const addToCart = (drink) => {
    124 +  if (!drink?.id) return
    125 +  const key = String(drink.id)
    126 +  if (!cart[key]) {
    127 +    cart[key] = {
    128 +      id: drink.id,
    129 +      name: drink.name,
    130 +      price: drink.price,
    131 +      imageUrl: drink.imageUrl,
    132 +      quantity: 0
    133 +    }
    134 +  }
    135 +  cart[key].quantity += 1
    136 +}
    137 +
    138 +const increment = (item) => addToCart(item)
    139 +
    140 +const decrement = (item) => {
    141 +  const key = String(item.id)
    142 +  if (!cart[key]) return
    143 +  cart[key].quantity -= 1
    144 +  if (cart[key].quantity <= 0) {
    145 +    delete cart[key]
    146 +  }
    147 +}
    148 +
    149 +const clearCart = () => {
    150 +  Object.keys(cart).forEach((key) => delete cart[key])
    151 +}
    152 +
    153 +const emitCheckout = () => {
    154 +  if (!cartItems.value.length) return
    155 +  emit('checkout', cartItems.value)
    156 +}
    157 +
    158 +const coverStyle = (image) => ({

    164 +const setCategory = (value) => {

    169 +  }
    170 +}

    142 +const preparedDrinks = computed(() =>

    150 +  }))

    153 +const catalog = computed(() => {
    154 +  const result = { CLASSIC: [], SIGNATURE: [], POUR: [] }

    156 +    const key = result[item.category] ? item.category : 'CLASSIC'
    157 +    result[key].push(item)
    158 +  })
    159 +  return result
    160 +})
    161 +
    162 +const currentProducts = computed(() => {
    163 +  if (activeCategory.value === 'DESSERT') return dessertList
    164 +  return catalog.value[activeCategory.value] || []
    165 +})
    166 +
    167 +const cartItems = computed(() => Object.values(cart))
    168 +const cartCount = computed(() => cartItems.value.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.quantity, 0))
    169 +const cartTotal = computed(() =>
    170 +  cartItems.value.reduce((sum, item) => sum + Number(item.price || 0) * item.quantity, 0)
    171 +)
    172 +
    173 +const coverStyle = (image) => ({
    174 +  backgroundImage: `linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(15,23,42,0.4), rgba(2,6,23,0.55)), url(${image})`
    175 +})

    179 +}
    180 +
    181 +const startSlide = () => {
    182 +  stopSlide()

    184 +    activeSlide.value = (activeSlide.value + 1) % heroSlides.length
    185 +  }, 4000)

    187 +

    191 +    slideTimer.value = null
    192 +  }
    193 +}

    195 +const selectCategory = (value) => {
    196 +  activeCategory.value = value
    197 +}
    198 +
    199 +const addProduct = (product) => {
    200 +  const id = product.id || product.name
    201 +  if (!cart[id]) {
    202 +    cart[id] = {
    203 +      id,
    204 +      name: product.name,
    205 +      price: Number(product.price || 0),
    206 +      quantity: 0
    207 +    }
    208 +  }
    209 +  cart[id].quantity += 1
    210 +}
    211 +
    212 +const increment = (item) => addProduct(item)
    213 +
    214 +const decrement = (item) => {
    215 +  const entry = cart[item.id]
    216 +  if (!entry) return
    217 +  entry.quantity -= 1
    218 +  if (entry.quantity <= 0) delete cart[item.id]
    219 +}
    220 +
    221 +const clearCart = () => {
    222 +  Object.keys(cart).forEach((key) => delete cart[key])
    223 +}
    224 +
    225 +const emitCheckout = () => {
    226 +  if (!cartItems.value.length) return
    227 +  emit('checkout', cartItems.value)
    228 +}

  <script setup>

  const emit = defineEmits(['checkout'])

  const heroSlides = [
    { tag: 'ç»å…¸æ¨è', title: 'ç„¦ç³–ç‡•éº¦æ‹¿é“', subtitle: 'ä¸æ»‘ç‡•éº¦å¥¶æ­é…æ·¡æ·¡ç„¦ç³–' },
    { tag: 'å­£èŠ‚é™å®š', title: 'èŠèŠé¾™äº•æ°”æ³¡', subtitle: 'èŒ¶é¦™æ°”æ³¡è®©æ¸…çˆ½åŠ å€' },
    { tag: 'æ‰‹ä½œç”œå“', title: 'çº¢èŒ¶æ— èŠ±æœå·´æ–¯å…‹', subtitle: 'èœœæ¸æ— èŠ±æœä¸é”¡å…°çº¢èŒ¶çš„ç¢°æ’' }
  ]

  const navItems = [
    { label: 'ç”œå“', value: 'DESSERT', icon: 'ğŸ°' },
    { label: 'ç»å…¸å’–å•¡', value: 'CLASSIC', icon: 'â˜•' },
    { label: 'ç‰¹è‰²æ‰‹å†²', value: 'POUR', icon: 'ğŸ«˜' },
    { label: 'ç‰¹è°ƒ', value: 'SIGNATURE', icon: 'ğŸ§ª' }
  ]

  const dessertList = [
    { id: 'fig-basque', name: 'çº¢èŒ¶æ— èŠ±æœå·´æ–¯å…‹', description: 'èœœæ¸æ— èŠ±æœæ­é…é”¡å…°çº¢èŒ¶ï¼Œå†·è—å£æ„Ÿæœ€ä½³ã€‚', price: 48,
  image: 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1504753793650-d4a2b783c15f?auto=format&fit=crop&w=600&q=80', tag: 'é™é‡' },
    { id: 'choco-basque', name: 'è¿ªæ‹œå·§å…‹åŠ›å·´æ–¯å…‹', description: '70% é»‘å·§ä¸æ¤°æ£ç³–æµ†å¸¦æ¥æµ“éƒå±‚æ¬¡ã€‚', price: 52, image:
  'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1505253399886-34b28f31c15f?auto=format&fit=crop&w=600&q=80', tag: 'äººæ°”' }
  ]

  const activeSlide = ref(0)
  const slideTimer = ref(null)
  const activeCategory = ref('DESSERT')
  const cart = reactive({})

  const preparedDrinks = computed(() =>
    props.drinks.map((drink, index) => ({
      id: drink.id ?? `drink-${index}`,
      name: drink.name ?? 'çµæ„Ÿé¥®å“',
      description: drink.description ?? 'è¿™æ¯é¥®å“æ­£ç­‰å¾…ä½ æ¥å®šä¹‰æ•…äº‹ã€‚',
      price: Number(drink.price || 0),
      image: drink.imageUrl || dessertList[index % dessertList.length].image,
      category: String(drink.category || '').toUpperCase()
    }))
  )

  const catalog = computed(() => {
    const result = { CLASSIC: [], SIGNATURE: [], POUR: [] }
    preparedDrinks.value.forEach((item) => {
      const key = result[item.category] ? item.category : 'CLASSIC'
      result[key].push(item)
    })
    return result
  })

  const currentProducts = computed(() => (activeCategory.value === 'DESSERT' ? dessertList :
  catalog.value[activeCategory.value] || []))
  const cartItems = computed(() => Object.values(cart))
  const cartCount = computed(() => cartItems.value.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.quantity, 0))
  const cartTotal = computed(() => cartItems.value.reduce((sum, item) => sum + Number(item.price || 0) * item.quantity,
  0))

  const coverStyle = (image) => ({
    backgroundImage: `linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(15,23,42,0.4), rgba(2,6,23,0.55)), url(${image})`
  })

  const setSlide = (index) => {
    activeSlide.value = index
  }

  const startSlide = () => {
    stopSlide()
    slideTimer.value = setInterval(() => {
      activeSlide.value = (activeSlide.value + 1) % heroSlides.length
    }, 4000)
  }

  const stopSlide = () => {
    if (slideTimer.value) {
      clearInterval(slideTimer.value)
      slideTimer.value = null
    }
  }

  const selectCategory = (value) => {
    activeCategory.value = value
  }

  const addProduct = (product) => {
    const id = product.id || product.name
    if (!cart[id]) {
      cart[id] = { id, name: product.name, price: Number(product.price || 0), quantity: 0 }
    }
    cart[id].quantity += 1
  }

  const increment = (item) => addProduct(item)
  const decrement = (item) => {
    const entry = cart[item.id]
    if (!entry) return
    entry.quantity -= 1

  const clearCart = () => Object.keys(cart).forEach((key) => delete cart[key])
  const emitCheckout = () => {
    if (!cartItems.value.length) return
    emit('checkout', cartItems.value)
  }

  onMounted(() => startSlide())
  onUnmounted(() => stopSlide())
  </script>

     97 +const activeCategory = ref(props.initialCategory || 'CLASSIC')
     98 +const contentRef = ref(null)
     99 +const cart = reactive({})
    100 +
    101 +const resolveCategory = (drink, index) => {
    102 +  const explicit = String(drink.category || drink.type || '').toUpperCase()
    103 +  if (navItems.some((item) => item.value === explicit)) return explicit
    104 +  const text = `${drink.name} ${drink.description || ''}`.toLowerCase()
    105 +  if (text.includes('æ‰‹å†²')) return 'POUR'
    106 +  if (text.includes('ç‰¹è°ƒ')) return 'SIGNATURE'
    107 +  if (text.includes('ç”œå“')) return 'DESSERT'
    108 +  return navItems[index % navItems.length].value
    109 +}
    110 +
    111 +const sections = computed(() =>
    112 +  navItems.map((item) => ({
    113 +    ...item,
    114 +    anchor: `section-${item.value.toLowerCase()}`,
    115 +    items: props.drinks.filter((drink, index) => resolveCategory(drink, index) === item.value)
    116 +  }))
    117 +)
    118 +
    119 +const cartItems = computed(() => Object.values(cart))
    120 +const cartTotal = computed(() =>
    121 +  cartItems.value.reduce((sum, item) => sum + Number(item.price || 0) * item.quantity, 0)
    122 +)
    123 +
    124 +const addToCart = (drink) => {
    125 +  if (!drink?.id) return
    126 +  const key = String(drink.id)
    127 +  if (!cart[key]) {

    220 +const addProduct = (product) => {

    237 +const decrement = (item) => {

    143 +const resolveCategory = (drink, index) => {
    144 +  const explicit = String(drink.category || drink.type || '').toUpperCase()

    146 +  const text = `${drink.name || ''} ${drink.description || ''}`.toLowerCase()

    189 +const addToCart = (drink) => {

    199 +    }
    200 +  }

    202 +}
    203 +
    204 +const increment = (item) => addToCart(item)
    205 +
    206 +const decrement = (item) => {
    207 +  const entry = cart[item.id]

    209 +  entry.quantity -= 1
    210 +  if (entry.quantity <= 0) {
    211 +    delete cart[item.id]
    212 +  }
    213 +}

    215 +const clearCart = () => {

    219 +const emitCheckout = () => {

    224 +const toggleCart = () => {
    225 +  cartOpen.value = !cartOpen.value
    226 +}

    228 +const updateDevice = () => {

    232 +    cartOpen.value = true
    233 +  }

    243 +  }

    245 +    cartOpen.value = true
